data-v-2e077fc1> This Privacy Policy describes Our policies and procedures on the collection, use and disclosure of Your information when You use the LabEx Service and tells You about Your privacy rights and how the law protects You. </p><p data-v-2e077fc1> We use your personal data to provide and improve the Service. By using the Service, You agree to the collection and use of information in accordance with this Privacy Policy. </p><h2 data-v-2e077fc1>Interpretation and Definitions</h2><h3 data-v-2e077fc1>Interpretation</h3><p data-v-2e077fc1> The words of which the initial letter is capitalized have meanings defined under the following conditions. The following definitions shall have the same meaning regardless of whether they appear in singular or in plural. </p><h3 data-v-2e077fc1>Definitions</h3><p data-v-2e077fc1>For the purposes of this Privacy Policy:</p><ul data-v-2e077fc1><li data-v-2e077fc1><span class="font-strong" data-v-2e077fc1>Account</span> means a unique account created for You to access our Service or parts of our Service. </li><li data-v-2e077fc1><span class="font-strong" data-v-2e077fc1>AI Assistant Labby:</span> An AI-powered tool provided as part of the Service, designed to assist users by offering guidance, answering queries, and facilitating the learning process within LabEx. </li><li data-v-2e077fc1><span class="font-strong" data-v-2e077fc1>Virtual Machine (VM):</span> A software emulation of a physical computer that runs an operating system and applications, providing a virtualized environment for users to perform and practice their lab exercises as part of the Service. </li><li data-v-2e077fc1><span class="font-strong" data-v-2e077fc1>Affiliate</span> means an entity that controls, is controlled by or is under common control with a party, where &quot;control&quot; means ownership of 50% or more of the shares, equity interest or other securities entitled to vote for election of directors or other managing authority. </li><li data-v-2e077fc1><span class="font-strong" data-v-2e077fc1>Company</span> (referred to as either &quot;the Company&quot;, &quot;We&quot;, &quot;Us&quot; or &quot;Our&quot; in this Agreement) refers to Chengdu Hangnolaibai Technology Co., Ltd., 6th floor W6, Global Center, No. 1700, Tianfu Road North, High-tech Zone, Chengdu. </li><li data-v-2e077fc1><span class="font-strong" data-v-2e077fc1>Cookies</span> are small files that are placed on Your computer, mobile device or any other device by a website, containing the details of Your browsing history on that website among its many uses. </li><li data-v-2e077fc1><span class="font-strong" data-v-2e077fc1>Country</span> refers to: China </li><li data-v-2e077fc1><span class="font-strong" data-v-2e077fc1>Device</span> means any device that can access the Service such as a computer, a cellphone or a digital tablet. </li><li data-v-2e077fc1><span class="font-strong" data-v-2e077fc1>Personal Data</span> is any information that relates to an identified or identifiable individual. </li><li data-v-2e077fc1><span class="font-strong" data-v-2e077fc1>Service</span> refers to the Website. </li><li data-v-2e077fc1><span class="font-strong" data-v-2e077fc1>Service Provider</span> means any natural or legal person who processes the data on behalf of the Company. It refers to third-party companies or individuals employed by the Company to facilitate the Service, to provide the Service on behalf of the Company, to perform services related to the Service or to assist the Company in analyzing how the Service is used. </li><li data-v-2e077fc1><span class="font-strong" data-v-2e077fc1> Third-party Social Media Service </span> refers to any website or any social network website through which a User can log in or create an account to use the Service. </li><li data-v-2e077fc1><span class="font-strong" data-v-2e077fc1>Usage Data</span> refers to data collected automatically, either generated by the use of the Service or from the Service infrastructure itself (for example, the duration of a page visit). </li><li data-v-2e077fc1><span class="font-strong" data-v-2e077fc1>Website</span> refers to LabEx, accessible from <a href="https://labex.io" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-v-2e077fc1>https://labex.io</a> . </li><li data-v-2e077fc1><span class="font-strong" data-v-2e077fc1>You</span> means the individual accessing or using the Service, or the company, or other legal entity on behalf of which such individual is accessing or using the Service, as applicable. </li></ul><h2 data-v-2e077fc1>Collecting and Using Your Personal Data</h2><h3 data-v-2e077fc1>Types of Data Collected</h3><h4 data-v-2e077fc1>Personal Data</h4><p data-v-2e077fc1> While using Our Service, We may ask You to provide Us with certain personally identifiable information that can be used to contact or identify You. Personally identifiable information may include, but is not limited to: </p><ul data-v-2e077fc1><li data-v-2e077fc1>Email address</li><li data-v-2e077fc1>First name and last name</li><li data-v-2e077fc1>Usage Data</li></ul><h4 data-v-2e077fc1>Usage Data</h4><p data-v-2e077fc1> Usage Data is collected automatically when using the Service. </p><p data-v-2e077fc1> Usage Data may include information such as Your Device&#39;s Internet Protocol address (e.g. IP address), browser type, browser version, the pages of our Service that You visit, the time and date of Your visit, the time spent on those pages, unique device identifiers and other diagnostic data. </p><p data-v-2e077fc1> When You access the Service by or through a mobile device, We may collect certain information automatically, including, but not limited to, the type of mobile device You use, Your mobile device unique ID, the IP address of Your mobile device, Your mobile operating system, the type of mobile Internet browser You use, unique device identifiers and other diagnostic data. </p><p data-v-2e077fc1> When using the LabEx platform, we collect specific types of Usage Data to enhance your learning experience and improve our services. This includes, but is not limited to: </p><ol data-v-2e077fc1><li data-v-2e077fc1> Interactions within Virtual Environments: We track inputs and operations performed in virtual lab environments. This helps us understand your learning patterns and improve lab functionalities. </li><li data-v-2e077fc1> Conversations with AI Assistant Labby: We record inputs and clicks during your interactions with our AI Assistant, Labby. This includes questions asked, options selected, and any feedback provided. These interactions are crucial for improving Labby&#39;s assistance capabilities and personalizing your learning journey. </li><li data-v-2e077fc1> AI-Generated Output Data: Information and responses generated by AI in response to your queries are also collected. This data helps us fine-tune our AI&#39;s accuracy and relevance to your learning needs. </li></ol><p data-v-2e077fc1> Please note that all Usage Data collected is subject to our comprehensive data security and privacy protocols. Our aim is to ensure a tailored and effective learning experience while upholding the highest standards of data privacy and security. </p><h4 data-v-2e077fc1>Information from Third-Party Social Media Services</h4><p data-v-2e077fc1> The Company allows You to create an account and log in to use the Service through the following Third-party Social Media Services: </p><ul data-v-2e077fc1><li data-v-2e077fc1>Google</li><li data-v-2e077fc1>Github</li></ul><p data-v-2e077fc1> If You decide to register through or otherwise grant us access to a Third-Party Social Media Service, We may collect Personal data that is already associated with Your Third-Party Social Media Service&#39;s account, such as Your name, Your email address, Your activities or Your contact list associated with that account. </p><p data-v-2e077fc1> You may also have the option of sharing additional information with the Company through Your Third-Party Social Media Service&#39;s account. If You choose to provide such information and Personal Data, during registration or otherwise, You are giving the Company permission to use, share, and store it in a manner consistent with this Privacy Policy. </p><h4 data-v-2e077fc1>Tracking Technologies and Cookies</h4><p data-v-2e077fc1> We use Cookies and similar tracking technologies to track the activity on Our Service and store certain information. Tracking technologies used are beacons, tags, and scripts to collect and track information and to improve and analyze Our Service. The technologies We use may include: </p><ul data-v-2e077fc1><li data-v-2e077fc1><span class="font-strong" data-v-2e077fc1>Cookies or Browser Cookies.</span> A cookie is a small file placed on Your Device. You can instruct Your browser to refuse all Cookies or to indicate when a Cookie is being sent. However, if You do not accept Cookies, You may not be able to use some parts of our Service. Unless you have adjusted Your browser setting so that it will refuse Cookies, our Service may use Cookies. </li><li data-v-2e077fc1><span class="font-strong" data-v-2e077fc1>Web Beacons.</span> Certain sections of our Service and our emails may contain small electronic files known as web beacons (also referred to as clear gifs, pixel tags, and single-pixel gifs) that permit the Company, for example, to count users who have visited those pages or opened an email and for other related website statistics (for example, recording the popularity of a certain section and verifying system and server integrity). </li></ul><p data-v-2e077fc1> Cookies can be &quot;Persistent&quot; or &quot;Session&quot; Cookies. Persistent Cookies remain on Your personal computer or mobile device when You go offline, while Session Cookies are deleted as soon as You close Your web browser. </p><p data-v-2e077fc1> We use both Session and Persistent Cookies for the purposes set out below: </p><ul data-v-2e077fc1><li data-v-2e077fc1><span class="font-strong" data-v-2e077fc1> Necessary / Essential Cookies </span></li><li data-v-2e077fc1>Type: Session Cookies</li><li data-v-2e077fc1>Administered by: Us</li><li data-v-2e077fc1> Purpose: These Cookies are essential to provide You with services available through the Website and to enable You to use some of its features. They help to authenticate users and prevent fraudulent use of user accounts. Without these Cookies, the services that You have asked for cannot be provided, and We only use these Cookies to provide You with those services. </li><li data-v-2e077fc1><span class="font-strong" data-v-2e077fc1> Cookies Policy / Notice Acceptance Cookies </span></li><li data-v-2e077fc1>Type: Persistent Cookies</li><li data-v-2e077fc1>Administered by: Us</li><li data-v-2e077fc1> Purpose: These Cookies identify if users have accepted the use of cookies on the Website. </li><li data-v-2e077fc1><span class="font-strong" data-v-2e077fc1>Functionality Cookies</span></li><li data-v-2e077fc1>Type: Persistent Cookies</li><li data-v-2e077fc1>Administered by: Us</li><li data-v-2e077fc1> Purpose: These Cookies allow us to remember choices You make when You use the Website, such as remembering your login details or language preference. The purpose of these Cookies is to provide You with a more personal experience and to avoid You having to re-enter your preferences every time You use the Website. </li></ul><p data-v-2e077fc1> For more information about the cookies we use and your choices regarding cookies, please visit our Cookies Policy or the Cookies section of our Privacy Policy. </p><h3 data-v-2e077fc1>Use of Your Personal Data</h3><p data-v-2e077fc1> The Company may use Personal Data for the following purposes: </p><ul data-v-2e077fc1><li data-v-2e077fc1><span class="font-strong" data-v-2e077fc1> To provide and maintain our Service </span> , including to monitor the usage of our Service. </li><li data-v-2e077fc1><span class="font-strong" data-v-2e077fc1>To manage Your Account:</span> to manage Your registration as a user of the Service. We will retain and use Your Personal Data to the extent necessary to comply with our legal obligations (for example, if we are required to retain your data to comply with applicable laws), resolve disputes, and enforce our legal agreements and policies. </p><p data-v-2e077fc1> The Company will also retain Usage Data for internal analysis purposes. Usage Data is generally retained for a shorter period of time, except when this data is used to strengthen the security or to improve the functionality of Our Service, or We are legally obligated to retain this data for longer time periods. </p><h3 data-v-2e077fc1>Transfer of Your Personal Data</h3><p data-v-2e077fc1> Your information, including Personal Data, is processed at the Company&#39;s operating offices and in any other places where the parties involved in the processing are located. It means that this information may be transferred to  and maintained on  computers located outside of Your state, province, country or other governmental jurisdiction where the data protection laws may differ than those from Your jurisdiction. </p><p data-v-2e077fc1> Your consent to this Privacy Policy followed by Your submission of such information represents Your agreement to that transfer. </p><p data-v-2e077fc1> The Company will take all steps reasonably necessary to ensure that Your data is treated securely and in accordance with this Privacy Policy and no transfer of Your Personal Data will take place to an organization or a country unless there are adequate controls in place including the security of Your data and other personal information. </p><h3 data-v-2e077fc1>Delete Your Personal Data</h3><p data-v-2e077fc1> You have the right to delete or request that We assist in deleting the Personal Data that We have collected about You. </p><p data-v-2e077fc1> Our Service may give You the ability to delete certain information about You from within the Service. </p><p data-v-2e077fc1> You may update, amend, or delete Your information at any time by signing in to Your Account, if you have one, and visiting the account settings section that allows you to manage Your personal information. We will provide notice before Your Personal Data is transferred and becomes subject to a different Privacy Policy. </p><h4 data-v-2e077fc1>Law enforcement</h4><p data-v-2e077fc1> Under certain circumstances, the Company may be required to disclose Your Personal Data if required to do so by law or in response to valid requests by public authorities (e.g. a court or a government agency). </p><h4 data-v-2e077fc1>Other legal requirements</h4><p data-v-2e077fc1> The Company may disclose Your Personal Data in the good faith belief that such action is necessary to: </p><ul data-v-2e077fc1><li data-v-2e077fc1>Comply with a legal obligation</li><li data-v-2e077fc1> Protect and defend the rights or property of the Company </li><li data-v-2e077fc1> Prevent or investigate possible wrongdoing in connection with the Service </li><li data-v-2e077fc1> Protect the personal safety of Users of the Service or the public </li><li data-v-2e077fc1>Protect against legal liability</li></ul><h3 data-v-2e077fc1>Security of Your Personal Data</h3><p data-v-2e077fc1> The security of Your Personal Data is important to Us, but remember that no method of transmission over the Internet, or method of electronic storage is 100% secure. While We strive to use commercially acceptable means to protect Your Personal Data, We cannot guarantee its absolute security. </p><h2 data-v-2e077fc1>Your Rights in Relation to Your Personal Information</h2><h3 data-v-2e077fc1>For Residents of the EEA or the UK</h3><p data-v-2e077fc1> As a resident of the European Economic Area (EEA) or the United Kingdom (UK), you are entitled to certain rights under the General Data Protection Regulation (GDPR) and UK GDPR, respectively. These include, under specific conditions: </p><ul data-v-2e077fc1><li data-v-2e077fc1>Access to a copy of your personal data held by us.</li><li data-v-2e077fc1> Request rectification or deletion of your personal data in our records. </li><li data-v-2e077fc1> Ask for restriction on processing your personal data (e.g., during verification of concerns). </li><li data-v-2e077fc1> Object to further processing of your personal data, including for marketing purposes. </li><li data-v-2e077fc1>Transfer your data to a third party.</li><li data-v-2e077fc1> File a complaint with relevant supervisory authorities. </li></ul><p data-v-2e077fc1> To exercise these rights, please email us or use the settings on your LabEx profile page. We may request additional information to verify your identity before fulfilling your request. Note that exceptions and limitations apply to each of these rights. Changes will be reflected in our active user databases promptly. We may retain personal data for backups, fraud prevention, legal obligations, or other legitimate reasons. </p><h3 data-v-2e077fc1>For United States Residents</h3><p data-v-2e077fc1> Residents of certain U.S. states, including California, Virginia, Colorado, Connecticut, and Utah, have specific privacy rights under state laws like the California Consumer Privacy Act (CCPA). If you reside in such states, your rights may include: </p><ul data-v-2e077fc1><li data-v-2e077fc1>Access to your personal data.</li><li data-v-2e077fc1> Details about our collection, use, disclosure, and handling of your personal data. </li><li data-v-2e077fc1>Deletion of personal data collected from you.</li><li data-v-2e077fc1> Opt-out of sharing or selling your personal data, where applicable. </li><li data-v-2e077fc1> Protection against discriminatory treatment for exercising your rights. </li></ul><p data-v-2e077fc1> To exercise these rights, you can email us or make adjustments on your LabEx profile page. We may ask for information to confirm your identity before fulfilling requests. </p><p data-v-2e077fc1><span class="font-strong" data-v-2e077fc1>CCPA Disclosure:</span> We do not sell personal information. Personal data may be shared with service providers (as defined by the CCPA) or disclosed to third parties as described in this policy and in accordance with U.S. state data privacy laws. </p><h2 data-v-2e077fc1>Links to Other Websites</h2><p data-v-2e077fc1> Our Service may contain links to other websites that are not operated by Us. If You click on a third party link, You will be directed to that third party&#39;s site.
